Lara (0)

Active To Narin!
Master Level 1
Description Return to Narin.
Level 1 MP Cost: 5. Moves you to Narin.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Active Shapeshift
Master Level 1
Description Hide your Anima horns to conceal where you're from.
Use the skill again to restore these features.
Not shown by default in some UI.
Level 1 Hide your horns.
Cooldown: 10 sec.


Active Exclusive Spell
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increase the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby characters.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: +4%, Duration: 40 min.


Passive Spirit Affinity
Master Level 1
Description Harness your natural affinity as an Anima to increase the duration of your summons.
Level 1 Minion Duration +10%


Passive Nature's Friend
Master Level 2
Description Receive help by becoming friends with the surrounding nature. Has an even greater effect on weak monsters, which are unable to withstand the power of nature.
Level 1 Damage: +3%
Activate nature's help upon defeating 20 normal monsters. Increases Damage Against Normal Monsters by 7% for 30 sec. when nature's help is active.
Cooldown: 30 sec.
2 Damage: +5%
Activate nature's help upon defeating 20 normal monsters. Increases Damage Against Normal Monsters by 11% for 30 sec. when nature's help is active.
Cooldown: 30 sec.

Lara (II)

Active Dragon Vein Reading
Master Level 1
Description Read the earth's pulse to discover the location of Dragon Veins containing the earth's essence. Dragon Veins are strongly imbued with one of the natural elements, and will hold the power of either the river, wind, or sun. Use Dragon Vein skills to harness the power of those Dragon Veins. Dragon Veins cannot be found in towns.
Can be toggled On/Off
Level 1 Discover Dragon Veins in Lara's surroundings. A max of 10 dragon vein(s) can be found on the map. When moving away from the Dragon Veins, they will disappear, starting with those farthest away.
Cooldown: 5 sec.


Active Dragon Vein Eruption
Master Level 1
Description Dragon Vein Skill
Consumes the surrounding Dragon Veins to cause the power dormant in the Dragon Veins to erupt. Land spirits that match the Dragon Veins' attributes will remain and frolic in the area of eruption. If an Eruption or Absorption skill of the same attribute is activated during an Eruption skill, the previously activated Eruption skill will end. Eruption skills prioritize unconstrained Dragon Veins. If there are no unconstrained Dragon Veins, the nearest Dragon Vein will be consumed first. You will not take damage even when attacking enemies with attack reflection. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion. The duration of Eruption skills is unaffected by an increase in Summons Duration, but their strength grows proportionately instead.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Activates an Eruption skill that matches the Dragon Vein's attribute.
Increases Damage by 1% per 2% increase in Summons Duration.
Cooldown: 0.3 sec.

Passive Eruption: Sunrise Well
Master Level 20
Description Dragon Vein Skill, Eruption Skill
Several Sunlight Spirits join together to combine into a frightening giant form, then scatter to cover the surroundings with lava. The lava area periodically creates volcanic bombs that attack enemies within the lava area. Volcanic bombs will first target any boss monsters within the area, starting with the boss with the highest HP.
Lv. 20+ required to learn Manifestation: Sunlight-Filled Ground.
Level 1 Giant Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 88%, Number of Attacks: 6. After attack, Lava Area Duration: 16 sec, Damage: 91% per 1 sec., Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 10
Periodically creates 4 volcanic bomb(s). Volcanic Bomb Damage: 57%, Number of Attacks: 3, Max Volcanic Bombs: 5. If several volcanic bombs hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second volcanic bomb and onwards: -10%. Damage Over Time for enemies hit by volcanic bombs: 22% damage for 8 sec.
20 Giant Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 145%, Number of Attacks: 6. After attack, Lava Area Duration: 16 sec, Damage: 110% per 1 sec., Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 10
Periodically creates 4 volcanic bomb(s). Volcanic Bomb Damage: 95%, Number of Attacks: 3, Max Volcanic Bombs: 5. If several volcanic bombs hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second volcanic bomb and onwards: -10%. Damage Over Time for enemies hit by volcanic bombs: 60% damage for 8 sec.

Active Mountain Seeds
Master Level 10
Description Plant seeds that grow a Mountain Spirits, who then attack nearby enemies and, if there is an active Eruption skill of any attribute within a certain range, will push enemies towards the Eruption skill. You will not take damage while using Mountain Seeds, even when attacking enemies with attack reflection.
Use Mountain Seeds while casting Dragon Vein Eruption to plant seeds without the casting motion, or use with the down arrow key to plant all the seeds at once. In Auto Mode, if seeds are prepared, a Mountain Seed will be planted in the location of a Dragon Vein each time an Eruption skill is used.
Auto Mode On/Off: Right-click
Level 1 MP Cost: 20. Mountain Spirit Duration: 10 sec., Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 28%, Number of Attacks: 1.
Max Mountain Spirits on Map: 4
1 Mountain Seed is recharged every 7 sec., and you can hold up to 4 at a time.

Active Manifestation: Where the River Courses
Master Level 20
Description Dragon Vein Skill, Manifestation Skill
Manifest the power of the river within a Dragon Vein to allow travel along the river's flow. Reuse the skill within a certain period of time to designate the river's end point. After designating an end point, the river will flow continuously between the start and end point, and Lara can press the up arrow key at the start point or end point to ride along the river. The end point cannot be designated at portal locations and certain other areas, and this skill cannot be used in some non-hunting maps. Manifestation skills prioritize unconstrained Dragon Veins. If there are no unconstrained Dragon Veins, the nearest Dragon Vein will be consumed first. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion. Riding the river allows you to use a skill that consumes Dragon Veins 1 time (excluding Manifestation: Where the River Courses), increases the usable range, and also allows you to use skills that consume dragon veins in proportion to the distance traveled. This skill is unaffected by Buff Freezer.
Required Skill: Eruption: Heaving River Lv. 20+
Lv. 20+ required to learn Nature Master.
Level 1 MP Cost: 80. Use the skill to designate an end point within 20 sec. River Duration between Start Point and End Point: 90 sec. Press the up arrow key at the start point to travel along the river.
Cooldown: 60 sec.
[Passive Effect: Heaving River Damage: +63%p]
20 MP Cost: 80. Use the skill to designate an end point within 20 sec. River Duration between Start Point and End Point: 90 sec. Press the up arrow key at the start point to travel along the river.
Cooldown: 60 sec.
[Passive Effect: Heaving River Damage: +120%p]

Active Manifestation: Wind Swing
Master Level 20
Description Dragon Vein Skill, Manifestation Skill
Manifest the power of the wind within a Dragon Vein to create an area with a continuous updraft. Provides a buff that temporarily increases Attack Speed, Speed, and Jump. Press the up arrow key and hold down jump in mid-air within the area to ride a swing, propelled by the wind, and float. Manifestation skills prioritize unconstrained Dragon Veins. If there are no unconstrained Dragon Veins, the nearest Dragon Vein will be consumed first. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
Right-click to toggle the mode for party member use ON/OFF.
Required Skill: Eruption: Whirlwind Lv. 20+
Lv. 20+ required to learn Nature Master.
Level 1 Cost: MP 80, Wind Swing Duration: 11 sec.
Area Buff: Attack Speed: +1 level, Speed: +20, Jump: +20
Buff Duration for Self: 44 sec, Buff Duration for Party Members: 1 sec.
Press the up arrow key and hold down jump in mid-air within the area of the wind swing to float midair for up to 4.5 sec.
Cooldown: 60 sec.
[Passive Effect: Whirlwind Damage: +16% points]
20 Cost: MP 80, Wind Swing Duration: 30 sec.
Area Buff: Attack Speed: +1 level, Speed: +20, Jump: +20
Buff Duration for Self: 120 sec, Buff Duration for Party Members: 20 sec.
Press the up arrow key and hold down jump in mid-air within the area of the wind swing to float midair for up to 4.5 sec.
Cooldown: 60 sec.

Active Wakeup Call
Master Level 20
Description Dragon Vein Skill
Awaken multiple dormant Dragon Veins in the area, all at once. The awakened Dragon Veins emanate intangible forces, which pursue and attack nearby enemies. Wakeup Call prioritizes normal Dragon Veins for consumption over unconstrained Dragon Veins, and is unaffected by attack reflection. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30. Creates as many intangible forces as there are enemies. Min Intangible Forces: 7, Max Intangible Forces: 12, Damage: 67% Number of Attacks: 4

Active Dragon Vein Traces
Master Level 5
Description Follows the Dragon Veins' traces. Use the Earthly Energy that periodically accumulates in your body to instantly move to a nearby Dragon Vein and attack nearby enemies. You can move in 8 directions, and the arrow keys can be used to discover any Dragon Veins in the corresponding direction first. Any unconstrained Dragon Veins within the area are prioritized. If there are none, you will be moved to the nearest regular Dragon Vein. You will not be moved to a Dragon Vein that is too close to your current location.
Level 1 MP Cost: 69. Uses 1 Earthly Energy. Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 380%, Number of Attacks: 2
1 Earthly Energy is recharged every 6 sec., and you can hold up to 4 at a time.
Cooldown: 1 sec.
5 MP Cost: 65. Uses 1 Earthly Energy. Max Enemies Hit: 5, Damage: 500%, Number of Attacks: 2
1 Earthly Energy is recharged every 6 sec., and you can hold up to 4 at a time.
Cooldown: 1 sec.

Lara (IV)

Active Dragon Vein Absorption
Master Level 1
Description Dragon Vein Skill
Consumes the surrounding dragon vein to absorb the dormant powers within. Lara absorbs the power of the dragon vein's attribute, and the land spirits of the absorbed attribute deal attacks when either Essence Sprinkle or Wakeup Call hit. If an Eruption skill of the same attribute is activated during an Absorption skill, the previously activated Absorption skill will end. Absorption skills prioritize unconstrained Dragon Veins. If there are no unconstrained Dragon Veins, the nearest Dragon Vein will be consumed first. You will not take damage even when attacking enemies with attack reflection. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
Required Skill: Lv. 1+ in one Absorption Skill.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Activates an Absorption skill that matches the target Dragon Vein's attribute.
Cooldown: 0.3 sec.

Description Dragon Vein Skill, Absorption Skill
When Essence Sprinkle hits, the Sunlight Spirits gather together to emit spheres of condensed sunlight that pursue and attack enemies. Fireballs will first target any boss monsters within the area. If there are multiple boss monsters, the boss with the highest HP will be targeted.

Active Dragon Vein Conversion
Master Level 1
Description Converts the attribute of the target Dragon Vein. The Dragon Vein's current attribute cannot be selected. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
Level 1 MP Cost: 80, Press directional keys within 3 sec of using the skill to convert the target Dragon Vein's attribute into a different attribute.
Cooldown: 1 sec., Increases cooldown by 6 sec when attribute conversion is successful.

Passive Nature Master
Master Level 10
Description Become one with nature to better wield its powers. Using Eruption skills allows you to draw out even greater potential from Dragon Veins, increasing the power of Eruption skills. Does not stack with 3rd job Manifestation skill passive effects.
Required Skills: Manifestation: Where the River Courses Lv. 20+, Manifestation: Wind Swing Lv. 20+, Manifestation: Sunlight Filled Ground Lv. 20+
Level 1 Eruption Skill Duration: 18 sec
Heaving River
Surge Max Enemies Hit: +2, Number of Attacks: +5, Damage: 525%. Periodically creates a big surge with Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 635%, Number of Attacks: 8. Max Surge Count: A normal surge and a big surge, for a total of 9.
Whirlwind
Increases whirlwind range, Max Enemies Hit: +4, Damage: 310%
Sunrise Well
Giant Max Enemies Hit: +4, Damage: 480%. Increases lava area creation range, Lava Area Damage: 285%, Volcanic Bomb Damage: 315%, Damage Over Time for enemies hit with volcanic bombs: 80%. Creates volcanic bombs more frequently, 5 at a time, up to 5 time(s).

Active Decent Combat Orders
Master Level 25
Description Temporarily increases all of your skill levels. Only 4th Job Skills can be increased beyond master level while other skills can only be increased to master level.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]

If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec

Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.

Master Level 25

Cooldown: 250 sec

Active Lotus Flower
Master Level 25
Description Summon a lotus flower with an auspicious power. When you are hit by a fatal attack within a certain range around the lotus, the blessing of the lotus allows you to be revived inside the lotus instead of dying. Cannot be used while the Heaven's Door buff is active. If you receive a Heaven's Door buff while the lotus is summoned, the lotus will disappear.
Level 1 MP Cost: 15% of Max MP, Lotus Summon Duration: 1655 sec.
Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.
Cooldown: 400 sec. Skill Cooldown upon successful revival: +1545 sec.

Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.
Cooldown: 400 sec. Skill Cooldown upon successful revival: +1425 sec.
30 MP Cost: 15% of Max MP, Lotus Summon Duration: 1800 sec.
Invincible for 3.5 sec. upon revival.
Cooldown: 400 sec. Skill Cooldown upon successful revival: +1400 sec.

Master Level 25
Description Moves you to a different dimension to reduce the damage you take. Use the skill again to return. While in Ethereal Form, you cannot use other skills.

Class-Specific Skills

Show/hide all levels
Active Big Stretch
Master Level 25
Description Dragon Vein Skill
Awaken multiple dormant Dragon Veins in the area, all at once. The awakened Dragon Veins emanate intangible forces, which pursue and attack nearby enemies. The intangible forces will first target any boss monsters within the area, targeting the boss with the highest HP first. If there are no boss monsters, the forces will target the monsters near each Dragon Vein instead. Big Stretch prioritizes normal Dragon Veins for consumption over unconstrained Dragon Veins, and is unaffected by attack reflection. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500. Awaken 4 Dragon Vein(s) within a certain range around another Dragon Vein.
Each awakened Dragon Vein creates 7 intangible force(s). Intangible Force Damage: 1144%, Number of Attacks: 5
If several intangible forces hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second force and onwards: -30%
Cooldown: 60 sec. Cooldown if awakened Dragon Vein count is less than the max number that can be awakened: -12 sec for each Dragon Vein that could be awakened
25 MP Cost: 500. Awaken 4 Dragon Vein(s) within a certain range around another Dragon Vein.
Each awakened Dragon Vein creates 7 intangible force(s). Intangible Force Damage: 2200%, Number of Attacks: 5
If several intangible forces hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second force and onwards: -30%
Cooldown: 60 sec. Cooldown if awakened Dragon Vein count is less than the max number that can be awakened: -12 sec for each Dragon Vein that could be awakened
30 MP Cost: 500. Awaken 4 Dragon Vein(s) within a certain range around another Dragon Vein.
Each awakened Dragon Vein creates 7 intangible force(s). Intangible Force Damage: 2420%, Number of Attacks: 5
If several intangible forces hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second force and onwards: -30%
Cooldown: 60 sec. Cooldown if awakened Dragon Vein count is less than the max number that can be awakened: -12 sec for each Dragon Vein that could be awakened

Active Winding Mountain Ridge
Master Level 25
Description Calls forth quirky Mountain Spirits who love to run. They'll then run amok throughout the area, attacking everything they bump into. If there are any boss monsters nearby, the Mountain Spirits will go after them first. The Mountain Spirits are unaffected by attack reflection. If there is no platform in the area for them to spring forth from, they can't be summoned in that area.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500. Summons 3 group(s) of Mountain Spirits within a certain range. Once summoned, they periodically run at enemies to attack. Group Summon Duration: 30 sec. Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 520%, Number of Attacks: 4. Running into enemies decreases running speed. Max Number of Attacks: 20 per group
Cooldown: 60 sec.
25 MP Cost: 500. Summons 3 group(s) of Mountain Spirits within a certain range. Once summoned, they periodically run at enemies to attack. Group Summon Duration: 30 sec. Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 1000%, Number of Attacks: 4. Running into enemies decreases running speed. Max Number of Attacks: 20 per group
Cooldown: 60 sec.
30 MP Cost: 500. Summons 3 group(s) of Mountain Spirits within a certain range. Once summoned, they periodically run at enemies to attack. Group Summon Duration: 30 sec. Max Enemies Hit: 6, Damage: 1100%, Number of Attacks: 4. Running into enemies decreases running speed. Max Number of Attacks: 20 per group
Cooldown: 60 sec.

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Active HEXA Dragon Vein Eruption
Master Level 30
Description Dragon Vein Skill
Consume the surrounding Dragon Veins to cause the power dormant in the Dragon Veins to erupt. Land spirits that match the Dragon Veins' attributes will remain and frolic in the area of eruption.
If an Eruption or Absorption skill of the same attribute is activated during an Eruption skill, the previously activated Eruption skill will end.
Eruption skills prioritize unconstrained Dragon Veins. If there are no unconstrained Dragon Veins, the nearest Dragon Vein will be consumed first. You will not take damage even when attacking enemies with attack reflection. Applies 100% Knockback Resistance during casting motion.
The duration of Eruption skills is unaffected by an increase in Summons Duration, but their strength grows proportionately instead.
Required Skill: Nature Master Lv. 10
Level 1 MP Cost: 56, Activates an Eruption skill that matches the Dragon Vein's attribute.
Increases Damage by 1% per 2% increase in Summons Duration.
Cooldown: 0.3 sec.
[Passive Effect: Absorption Skill Final Damage: +7%]
30 MP Cost: 60, Activates an Eruption skill that matches the Dragon Vein's attribute.
Increases Damage by 1% per 2% increase in Summons Duration.
Cooldown: 0.3 sec.
[Passive Effect: Absorption Skill Final Damage: +21%]

Active HEXA Eruption: Sunrise Well
Master Level 30
Description Dragon Vein Skill, Eruption Skill
Several Sunlight Spirits join together to combine into a frightening giant form, then scatter to cover the surroundings with lava.
The lava area periodically creates volcanic bombs that attack enemies within the lava area. Volcanic bombs will first target the boss with the highest Max HP.
Required Skill: Nature Master Lv. 10
Level 1 Giant Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 770%, Number of Attacks: 6
After attack, Lava Area Duration: 18 sec
Damage: 455% per 1 sec, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 10
Periodically creates 5 volcanic bomb(s), Volcanic Bomb Damage: 472%, Number of Attacks: 3
Max Volcanic Bombs: 5, If several volcanic bombs hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second volcanic bomb and onwards: -10%.
Damage Over Time for enemies hit by volcanic bombs: 137% damage for 8 sec.
30 Giant Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 1060%, Number of Attacks: 6
After attack, Lava Area Duration: 18 sec
Damage: 600% per 1 sec, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 10
Periodically creates 5 volcanic bomb(s), Volcanic Bomb Damage: 675%, Number of Attacks: 3
Max Volcanic Bombs: 5, If several volcanic bombs hit a single enemy, Final Damage for the second volcanic bomb and onwards: -10%.
Damage Over Time for enemies hit by volcanic bombs: 195% damage for 8 sec.

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
